Publish Tickets Online with Confidence, Event Booking Plus
May 25, 2026
Getting people through the door starts long before event day. It begins the moment someone discovers your event, clicks on it, and decides whether to buy a ticket. That split-second decision depends on how smooth, secure, and professional the booking experience feels.
Event Booking Plus empowers organizers with powerful ticket management features that make it easy to create, customize, and control every aspect of ticket sales. From paid and free tickets to multiple ticket types, pricing, quantity limits, scheduled availability, and attendee data collection, the platform helps organizers manage tickets with confidence and flexibility.
With Event Booking Plus, publishing tickets online is simple, efficient, and built for results. Whether you are organizing a corporate conference, charity fundraiser, music festival, community workshop, or private event, the platform gives you complete control from setup to sale to check-in. Organizers can create event pages, share booking links, manage orders, collect customer details, send ticket confirmations, and streamline attendee entry with QR-based check-in.
By simplifying operations and enhancing the booking experience, Event Booking Plus helps deliver a seamless, professional journey for attendees. The result is stronger trust, smoother conversions, better event control, and a successful start before the event even begins.
Key Features
Streamlined Ticket Management
Create versatile ticket types with customizable pricing, availability, and quantity constraints. Offer diverse options like VIP, General Admission, or Early Bird to cater to varied attendee preferences.
Ticket Tailoring and Personalization
Tailor ticket specifics such as pricing, availability, and descriptions to suit evolving event needs. Personalise ticket aesthetics and brand elements to harmonise with event themes and branding.
Dynamic ticket control
Halt or restart ticket transactions to modulate entry limits and supervise event turnout. Pause ticket sales temporarily to implement alterations or cater to event logistics.
Benefits
Simplified Ticket Setup
Streamline the ticket creation process with easy-to-use tools and intuitive interfaces. Create a variety of ticket types to meet the needs and preferences of different attendee groups.
Enhanced Ticket Customization
Customise ticket details and designs to create a unique and engaging ticketing experience for attendees. Easily make changes to ticket information to reflect updates or modifications to event plans.
Controlled Ticket Sales
Maintain control over ticket availability and sales with the ability to pause or resume ticketing as needed. Manage event capacity and ensure a seamless ticketing experience for attendees.
Secure & Seamless Payment Experience
A smooth checkout process builds trust and drives more conversions. Event Booking Plus ensures secure payment processing with a seamless user experience, allowing attendees to book tickets quickly and confidently. With reliable payment integration and hassle-free transactions, you can reduce drop-offs and maximize ticket sales without worrying about technical issues or security concerns.
FAQs
How do I publish tickets online using Event Booking Plus?
Publishing tickets with Event Booking Plus is a straightforward, step-by-step process. Once you’re logged into your organizer dashboard, you can create your event, add ticket types, configure pricing and availability, personalize the ticket design, and publish,  all within minutes. There’s no technical knowledge required, and your tickets go live instantly once you’re ready.
Can I create multiple ticket types for the same event?
Yes, absolutely. Event Booking Plus supports multiple ticket categories under a single event, including VIP, General Admission, Early Bird, and group packages. Each ticket type has its own independent pricing, quantity limit, and availability window, giving you the flexibility to cater to different attendee segments without any overlap or confusion.
Can I pause or stop ticket sales after they go live?
Yes, and this is one of our most popular features among event organizers. You can pause ticket sales at any point,  whether you’ve hit your venue capacity, need to make an event update, or simply want to control the flow of registrations. Once you’re ready to resume, ticket sales can be switched back on instantly with a single click.
Can I customize how my event tickets look?
Definitely. Ticket customization is built into the core of Event Booking Plus. You can edit ticket titles, pricing, descriptions, and availability dates at any time. Visual and brand elements can also be tailored to reflect your event’s identity, helping create a professional and consistent experience for your attendees from the moment they land on your ticketing page.
Is there a limit to how many tickets I can publish per event?
You’re in full control of that. Event Booking Plus lets you set individual quantity caps for each ticket type, so you never have to worry about overselling or exceeding your venue capacity. When a ticket tier sells out, it’s automatically marked as unavailable,  keeping the experience clean for buyers.

Event Booking Plus offers a robust suite of event management features designed to simplify the process of organising and promoting events. From creating and publishing events to managing event details and sharing them across various platforms, Event Booking Plus provides all the tools you need to ensure your events are successful.
Running a successful event takes more than just a great idea, it requires the right tools, streamlined workflows, and a reliable platform to bring everything together. That’s exactly what Event Booking Plus is built for. Whether you’re planning a small community workshop or a large-scale corporate conference, the manage events feature gives you complete control, from the first draft of your event to the final headcount.
If you’ve ever felt overwhelmed juggling event details across spreadsheets, email threads, and disconnected apps, you’re not alone. Many event organizers face the same challenges. Event Booking Plus eliminates this chaos by providing a centralized platform where you can manage every aspect of your event planning and execution with ease.
Key Features
Event Creation and Customization
Effortlessly create bespoke events with personalised branding and thematic integration. Tailor each event page with sophisticated customization options for a distinctive touch.
Publishing and Sharing Events
Effortlessly showcase events on dedicated pages with enhanced visibility features for greater exposure. Share event URLs via social media platforms to widen reach and augment attendance.
Efficient Event Management
Leverage a sophisticated event dashboard for centralised event administration. Effortlessly refine event particulars, revise dates, and seamlessly track progress.
Seamless Event Promotion
Generate distinct event URLs for effortless dissemination across diverse platforms. Amplify event visibility by circulating URLs through social media channels to optimise reach and engagement.
Benefits
Streamlined Event Setup
Save significant time and effort with Event Booking Plus intuitive event creation and customization tools, allowing for quick and hassle-free event setup. Benefit from centralised event management features, ensuring seamless coordination and execution of all aspects of your event, saving you from the hassle of juggling multiple tools or platforms.
Enhanced Event Visibility
Boost event visibility through user-friendly event pages designed for increased exposure, eliminating the need for additional marketing efforts and reaching a broader audience effortlessly. Expand your event’s reach by easily sharing event URLs across various social media platforms, maximising visibility and attendance with minimal effort on your part.

Maintain control over all event details from a centralised dashboard, allowing for easy updates and modifications. Quickly adapt to changes by editing event details and managing event schedules effortlessly.
Save Time with a Centralized Workflow
One of the biggest challenges in event planning is managing tasks across multiple tools. Event Booking Plus eliminates this problem by bringing everything into one centralized system.
From event creation and promotion to updates and tracking, every action happens in one place. This reduces errors, improves coordination, and ensures your team stays aligned throughout the entire process.
Built for Growth and Scalability

Frequently Asked Questions, Manage Events
Q1. What does the Manage Events feature in Event Booking Plus include?
The Manage Events feature in Event Booking Plus covers everything you need to run a successful event , from creating and customizing your event page to publishing, promoting, and tracking it in real time. You get a centralized event dashboard where you can update event details, manage schedules, monitor registrations, and share your event across multiple channels, all from one place.
Q2. Do I need technical skills to create and manage events on Event Booking Plus?
Not at all. Event Booking Plus is designed to be user-friendly for everyone, regardless of technical background. The event creation process is straightforward and intuitive ,  you simply enter your event details, apply
your branding, and publish. No coding or design experience is required to get a professional-looking event page up and running in minutes.
Q3. Can I customize my event page to match my brand?
Yes. Event Booking Plus gives you full control over how your event page looks and feels. You can incorporate your brand colors, themes, logos, and personalized messaging to create a distinctive event experience. Q4. How do I share my event with a wider audience?

The more channels you share it on, the broader your reach and the higher your potential attendance.

This makes it especially useful for organizations that run recurring events, seasonal campaigns, or events across different locations.

Maximizing Ticket Sales: Using AI-Driven Dynamic Pricing for Music Festivals
May 25, 2026
Selling tickets for a music festival is exciting, but it can also be unpredictable. Some tickets sell quickly. Others move slowly. Early demand may look strong, but sales can drop closer to the event. For organizers, the challenge is simple: how do you price tickets in a way that attracts attendees, protects revenue, and avoids last-minute panic?
That is where
AI-driven dynamic pricing
can make a major difference.
Instead of using one fixed ticket price from launch to event day, dynamic pricing allows organizers to adjust ticket prices based on demand, availability, booking behavior, sales timing, and event performance. When used correctly, it helps music festivals sell more tickets, reduce empty seats, and improve overall revenue.
Event Booking Plus
, we help event organizers manage ticket sales, attendee data, secure payments, check-ins, seating, and event insights from one easy-to-use platform. For music festivals, this creates a smarter way to plan, sell, track, and optimize every stage of the ticketing process.
Why Music Festival Ticket Pricing Needs a Smarter Approach
Music festivals are not like regular events. They often include multiple ticket categories, early bird offers, VIP passes, group tickets, artist-based demand, seating zones, limited-capacity areas, and fast-changing audience interest.
A flat pricing strategy may seem simple, but it can limit your results.
For example:
If tickets are priced too low, you may sell out early but lose potential revenue.
If tickets are priced too high, interested attendees may delay or abandon their purchase.
If ticket sales slow down, you may need discounts at the last minute.
If demand suddenly increases, fixed pricing may prevent you from capturing higher-value bookings.
Dynamic pricing gives organizers more flexibility. It helps you respond to real demand instead of guessing what attendees might pay.
What Is AI-Driven Dynamic Pricing?
AI-driven dynamic pricing uses data and smart automation to recommend or adjust ticket prices based on real-time conditions. For music festivals, this can include:
Ticket sales speed
Remaining ticket quantity
Booking dates
Event popularity
Seat or zone availability
Ticket type demand
Attendee purchase behavior
Time left before the event
Festival lineup announcements
Historical sales patterns
The goal is not simply to raise prices. The goal is to use the right price at the right time for the right audience.
For example, early bird tickets may start at a lower price to build momentum. As more people book, prices can gradually increase. If VIP tickets are selling faster than general admission, VIP pricing can be reviewed separately. If a certain ticket category is moving slowly, organizers can adjust promotions or availability before it becomes a problem.
How Event Booking Plus Supports Smarter Ticket Sales
Event Booking Plus gives organizers the tools they need to manage ticket sales with structure and clarity. From creating event pages to tracking orders and attendee activity, everything stays organized in one centralized dashboard.
For music festival organizers, this means better control over the full ticketing journey.
Create Multiple Ticket Types for Different Festival Audiences
Every music festival has different attendee groups. Some people want basic entry. Others want premium access, better seating, backstage experiences, or group passes.
With Event Booking Plus, organizers can create different ticket types with details such as:
Ticket name
Ticket price
Available quantity
Ticket description
Booking start date
Booking end date
Maximum booking limits per person
This flexibility allows you to build a pricing structure that matches your festival experience.
For example, you can create:
Early bird general admission tickets
Regular general admission tickets
VIP passes
Student passes
Group tickets
Premium seating tickets
One-day or multi-day passes
By separating ticket types clearly, you can understand which audience segments are responding best and adjust your pricing strategy accordingly.
Use Booking Availability Dates to Build Urgency
One of the most useful features for ticket sales is scheduled booking availability. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to control when specific tickets become available for booking.
This is especially helpful for music festivals because ticket sales often happen in phases.
You can launch early bird tickets first, close them after a certain date, then open standard pricing. Later, you can introduce final-phase tickets or limited premium passes.
This creates urgency without confusing attendees.
For example:
Phase 1:
Early bird tickets available for the first two weeks
Phase 2:
Standard tickets available after early bird sells out
Phase 3:
Last-chance tickets available closer to the festival date
When attendees know prices or availability may change, they are more likely to book earlier.
Improve Revenue With Demand-Based Ticket Controls
Dynamic pricing works best when combined with smart ticket controls. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to set ticket quantities and booking limits, helping prevent overselling and improving attendance planning.
For high-demand music festivals, this is important because ticket scarcity can influence buying behavior. If attendees see limited availability for a popular ticket type, they may complete their purchase sooner.
At the same time, organizers can protect capacity by limiting how many tickets one person can book. This helps reduce bulk buying issues and keeps access fair for more attendees.
Support Assigned Seating for Premium Festival Experiences
Some music festivals include auditorium events, VIP zones, theatre-style performances, or reserved seating areas. Event Booking Plus includes seat selection functionality for events that require assigned seating.
When enabled, attendees can choose their seats from a seating map during the booking process.
This can help organizers create higher-value ticket categories such as:
Front-row seating
Premium viewing areas
Reserved VIP sections
Balcony or zone-based seating
Special access sections
Seat selection also improves the attendee experience because guests feel more in control of their booking.
Make the Booking Experience Simple for Attendees
A strong pricing strategy will not work if the booking process feels complicated. Attendees should be able to find the event, choose a ticket, enter their details, and complete payment without unnecessary steps.
Each event created in Event Booking Plus comes with a dedicated event page that can be shared through websites, email, social media, ads, or direct links.
The event page can display:
Event title and description
Date and time
Location details
Available ticket types
Seat selection if required
Maps
Social media links
Booking details
A clean event page helps reduce confusion and increases the chances of completed ticket purchases.
Secure Checkout Builds Buyer Confidence
Payment trust matters, especially for paid music festivals. Attendees want to know that their booking is safe and that they will receive proper confirmation after payment.
Event Booking Plus supports a smooth checkout process where attendees can review their booking summary, ticket pricing, fees, and taxes before completing payment.
After a successful booking, the platform records the order and sends ticket details to the attendee by email. This reduces manual work for organizers and gives attendees immediate confidence that their purchase is confirmed.
Track Orders, Attendee Records, and Sales Performance
AI-driven dynamic pricing depends on data. Without clear sales information, it is difficult to know whether your pricing strategy is working.
Event Booking Plus helps organizers track completed bookings through the Orders section. This includes attendee details, ticket information, seat selection details where applicable, payment status, and other booking information.
For festival organizers, this data can help answer important questions:
Which ticket type is selling fastest?
Are VIP tickets performing better than general admission?
Are attendees booking early or waiting?
Which ticket categories need promotion?
How many seats or tickets are still available?
Is the event on track to reach attendance goals?
These insights help organizers make smarter decisions before, during, and after the event.
Use Attendee Data to Improve Future Festival Planning
Ticket sales are only one part of festival success. The attendee data collected during booking can help organizers improve future events.
Event Booking Plus allows custom questions to be added during the booking process and assigned to specific ticket types. This is useful for collecting details such as preferences, access needs, membership information, food choices, or special requests.
For music festivals, custom questions can help you better understand your audience and personalize future marketing campaigns.
Speed Up Entry With QR-Based Check-Ins
A sold-out festival is only successful if entry management runs smoothly. Long lines, manual verification, and check-in delays can hurt the attendee experience.
Event Booking Plus supports QR code-based check-ins. When a ticket QR code is scanned, the attendee can be marked as present. This helps organizers verify guests faster and track real attendance accurately.
Attendance data can also help compare ticket sales with actual turnout, which is valuable for planning future festivals.
Why Event Booking Plus Is Ideal for Music Festival Organizers
Event Booking Plus is built to help organizers manage events from start to finish. For music festivals, it brings together the essential tools needed to sell tickets, manage bookings, track attendees, process payments, and improve event performance.
With Event Booking Plus, organizers can:
Create professional event pages
Manage multiple ticket types
Schedule ticket availability
Control ticket quantities
Offer seat selection
Collect attendee information
Process secure payments
Send ticket emails automatically
Track orders and attendance
Use event insights for better decisions
Instead of relying on spreadsheets, manual updates, and disconnected tools, organizers can manage everything from one structured platform.
AI-driven dynamic pricing can help music festival organizers move beyond guesswork. By combining flexible ticket setup, booking controls, attendee data, secure checkout, and performance insights, organizers can make smarter pricing decisions and create a smoother booking experience.
With
Event Booking Plus
, music festival organizers get more than a ticketing tool. They get a complete event management platform designed to support every stage of the event journey — from ticket launch to attendee check-in and post-event analysis.
If your goal is to sell more tickets, manage demand better, and deliver a professional festival experience, Event Booking Plus gives you the tools to make it happen.
FAQs
1. What is AI-driven dynamic pricing for music festivals?
AI-driven dynamic pricing is a ticket pricing strategy where prices can change based on factors such as demand, ticket availability, sales speed, booking dates, and attendee behavior. It helps festival organizers price tickets more effectively instead of using one fixed price throughout the entire sales period.
2. How can Event Booking Plus help increase music festival ticket sales?
Event Booking Plus helps organizers create event pages, manage multiple ticket types, schedule booking availability, track orders, collect attendee details, process secure payments, and monitor event performance. These tools make it easier to manage ticket sales and improve booking results.
3. Can I create early bird, VIP, and general admission tickets in Event Booking Plus?
Yes. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to create multiple ticket types with different names, prices, quantities, descriptions, and booking availability dates. This makes it suitable for early bird tickets, VIP passes, general admission, group tickets, and premium seating options.
4. Does Event Booking Plus support seat selection for music festivals?
Yes. Event Booking Plus includes seat selection functionality for events that require assigned seating. This is useful for auditorium events, premium festival zones, VIP seating, conferences, and theatre-style performances.
5. How does Event Booking Plus manage attendee check-ins?
Event Booking Plus supports attendee check-ins through event dashboards and QR code-based ticket scanning. When an attendee’s ticket QR code is scanned, they can be marked as present, helping organizers manage entry faster and track attendance accurately.

How to Scale Your Startup Event: A Guide to Seamless Multi-City Roadshows
May 25, 2026
So, your first event was a hit. Now you’re thinking bigger ,  literally. Taking your startup event on the road to multiple cities is a powerful way to grow your brand, connect with new audiences, and build real momentum.
But let’s be honest: a multi-city roadshow isn’t just “the same event repeated several times.” It’s a logistical puzzle. Different venues, ticket structures, attendee expectations, and on-the-ground operations can quickly become difficult to manage.
That’s where
Event Booking Plus
comes in. We help startups manage every part of the process ,  from creating city-specific event pages to tracking check-ins and collecting attendee insights ,  all from one centralized dashboard.
No spreadsheets. No missed details. Just smooth, scalable roadshows.
Why a Multi-City Roadshow Is a Game-Changer for Startups
Think of a roadshow as your startup’s mobile stage. It allows you to show up where your customers, investors, and partners actually are. Instead of relying only on digital campaigns, you create face-to-face connections that build trust and drive action.
Key benefits of a startup roadshow include:
Launching products in new markets with real-time feedback
Building investor and partner relationships beyond your home base
Running local customer education sessions that resonate
Generating qualified leads in multiple regions at once
Collecting authentic attendee insights you can’t get from a form alone
But here’s the catch: each new city adds complexity. Different ticket types, local taxes, seating layouts, and check-in workflows can overwhelm even the most organized team.
That’s why you need a platform designed for scale ,  not just for a single event.
1. Start With a Clear, Replicable Event Structure
Before you create a single event page, map out your roadshow’s core structure. Are you running the exact same agenda in every city, or will you adjust it based on the local audience, venue, or market needs?
Typical roadshow components may include:
Keynote session
Product demo or live walkthrough
Networking or meet-the-founder hour
Investor roundtable or pitch session
VIP ticket category with limited access
Free general admission tickets for lead generation
With
Event Booking Plus
, you can create multiple events under one organizer profile. Each city gets its own dedicated event page, while you manage everything from a single, intuitive dashboard.
Pro tip:
Use organizer-level profiles to separate events by region, team, or campaign type. This is especially useful for agencies or startups with distributed teams.
2. Build a Dedicated Event Page for Every City
Nothing confuses attendees more than landing on a generic “roadshow page” with vague location details. Each city in your roadshow deserves its own clear, shareable event page.
With Event Booking Plus, every event page can include:
Event title and compelling description
Start and end dates with timezone clarity
Venue address and map link
Available ticket types with pricing
Social media links for easy sharing
Custom branding options
Once created, each event appears as a card in your dashboard. You can click into any city to access its dedicated event dashboard, where you’ll manage tickets, orders, check-ins, surveys, and more.
No digging through messy folders. No confusion about which event belongs to which city.
3. Simplify Ticket Creation and Sales Across Cities
Ticket management can make or break your roadshow. Some cities may sell out quickly, while others may need early-bird discounts or free community tickets. You need flexibility ,  and you need it fast.
Event Booking Plus gives you per-ticket control over:
Ticket name and price, including free tickets
Quantity available
Ticket description
Booking availability window
Maximum tickets per person
Optional seat selection
Want tickets to go live the moment your campaign launches? Schedule them in advance. Need to offer member-only pricing? Create a separate ticket type and limit availability.
For paid events, the platform can calculate taxes and service fees and display a clear booking summary before checkout.
4. Handle Seat Selection When Your Venue Requires It
Not every roadshow event needs assigned seating. But if you’re hosting in an auditorium, theater, or conference hall with reserved sections, seat selection becomes essential.
Event Booking Plus includes interactive seat maps where attendees can choose their exact seat during checkout. This is ideal for:
VIP sections at product launches
Paid seminars or workshops
Investor dinners with assigned tables
Events where seating order matters
If seat selection isn’t needed, you can keep things simple with standard entry tickets. The choice is yours for each event.
5. Collect Attendee Data That Actually Matters
For startups, attendee data is valuable. A name and email address are just the starting point. You may also need to know company size, job role, investment interest, product feedback, or other details that support your next move.
With custom surveys and questions in Event Booking Plus, you can ask:
“What’s your biggest challenge in this industry?”
“Are you interested in a follow-up demo?”
“What’s your company’s current funding stage?”
“Do you have any dietary restrictions or accessibility needs?”
You can assign questions to specific ticket types. For example, you can ask VIP ticket holders for their LinkedIn profiles, while free attendees only provide basic contact details.
All answers are stored in attendee records, ready for export or CRM integration.
6. Streamline Check-Ins With QR Code Scanning
The day of the event should be about connecting with attendees, not managing clipboards. Manual check-ins are slow, error-prone, and can create a poor first impression.
Event Booking Plus generates a unique QR code for every ticket email. When attendees arrive, your team can scan the code from a phone or printed ticket, and the system instantly marks them as attended.
Benefits include:
No more guesswork about who showed up
Faster entry lines
Real-time attendance data across all cities
Reduced staffing needs at the door
More accurate event reporting
Think of it like airport check-in ,  but simpler, faster, and built for your event team.
7. Learn and Improve With Every Roadshow Stop
A multi-city roadshow shouldn’t be a guessing game. You need to know what worked in one city so you can improve the next stop.
Event Booking Plus provides dashboard insights on:
Which city had the highest ticket sales
Which ticket type performed best
Actual check-in rates compared to bookings
Most useful survey responses
Peak booking times to optimize marketing
These analytics help you refine everything from pricing and session length to venue selection and follow-up strategy. Each stop becomes smarter than the last.
Why Event Booking Plus Is Built for Startup Roadshows
Event Booking Plus is more than a basic ticketing tool. It is a complete event management platform designed for organizers who want to scale without operational stress.
Feature
How It Helps Your Roadshow

City-specific event pages
Create clear, local, shareable event URLs

Support flexible models for different markets

Keep all booking information in one place

Ready to Scale Your Startup Event?
You don’t need a massive operations team to run a successful multi-city roadshow. You need the right system.
Event Booking Plus helps you save time, reduce manual work, and focus on what matters most: creating memorable experiences in every city you visit.
Start your free trial today or schedule a demo to see how Event Booking Plus helps startups grow from one event to many.
Frequently Asked Questions
1. What’s the best way to manage a multi-city startup roadshow?
The best way is to use an all-in-one event management platform like Event Booking Plus. You can create separate event pages for each city, manage tickets and orders from one dashboard, track check-ins with QR codes, and collect attendee data without juggling spreadsheets or multiple tools.
2. Can I sell both paid and free tickets for different cities in the same roadshow?
Yes. Event Booking Plus supports paid tickets, free tickets, and flexible ticket options. You can customize ticket types for each city based on your goals, whether you’re focused on lead generation, revenue, or VIP access.
3. How does QR code check-in work for multi-city events?
Each attendee receives a unique QR code with their ticket. At the venue, your team scans the code using a smartphone or tablet. The system verifies the ticket and marks the attendee as present, helping you track check-ins across all cities.
4. Can I collect custom information from attendees during registration?
Yes. Event Booking Plus allows you to create custom survey questions and assign them to specific ticket types. For example, you can ask VIP ticket holders for dietary restrictions or ask investors about their business interests.
5. What if I need to change event details after publishing?
You can update event details after publishing. Use the customization options to edit event titles, descriptions, dates, venue addresses, ticket availability, and more. Changes can be updated without rebuilding the event page.
Event Booking Plus ,  built for organizers who think big. Start your multi-city journey today.

Why Event Booking Plus Is the Smartest Choice for Small Businesses in India: 2026 Guide
May 25, 2026
Let’s be honest: running an event as a small business in India is a juggling act. You are not just managing a venue and guests. You are handling workshop registrations, corporate meetup RSVPs, music show ticketing, and post-event follow-ups, often with a lean team and a tight budget.
The old way of relying on WhatsApp messages, spreadsheets, and offline payments can quickly become a nightmare. What you need is a reliable, all-in-one system. You need event management software for small businesses in India that can handle registrations, ticket sales, payments, and check-ins without requiring technical expertise.
That is where Event Booking Plus comes in. We are not just a generic tool; we are your digital partner in creating unforgettable experiences, from the first click to the final check-in.
Why Small Indian Businesses Are Upgrading Their Event Tech in 2026
The Indian event landscape has evolved. In 2026, your audience expects speed, transparency, and a digital-first experience. Manual processes create friction, and friction can cost you attendees.
A modern event management platform helps you:
Create professional, shareable event pages in minutes
Sell both free and paid tickets online with ease
Manage multiple organizers, clients, and events from one dashboard
Automate ticket confirmations and QR code delivery
Track real-time sales, attendance, and customer data
Speed up entry with QR code check-ins
“Event management software acts as the digital backbone that helps planners organize, execute, and measure events from a single platform.” – Guidebook
With Event Booking Plus, this backbone is built specifically for the needs of Indian small businesses, startups, and community builders.
8 Non-Negotiable Features Every Small Business Needs
Before choosing a platform, compare it against these real-world needs. Here is how Event Booking Plus stacks up.
1. Effortless Event Creation Without Coding
You should not need a developer to launch an event. Event Booking Plus lets you add your event title, description, dates, venue address, ticket details, and social media links in just a few clicks.
The EBP Advantage:
Create an organizer profile once and manage multiple events under it. This is perfect if you manage events for several clients, departments, or internal teams.
2. Flexible Paid and Free Ticketing
Not every event needs a paid ticket. Sometimes it is a free community gathering; other times it is a premium workshop with VIP access.
The EBP Advantage:
Create multiple ticket types such as Early Bird, General Entry, VIP, or Member-Only. You can set quantities, availability dates, and ticket limits per person for both free and paid events.
3. Frictionless Booking Without Login Barriers
Forcing attendees to create an account before booking is one of the fastest ways to lose registrations.
The EBP Advantage:
Share your public event URL on WhatsApp, Instagram, email, or your website. Users can select tickets, enter their details, and complete payment without needing to create an account, log in, or go through unnecessary steps. This helps improve the booking experience and can increase conversions.
4. Smart Seat Selection for Auditorium Events
Selling seats for a theatre show, conference, or cultural event? A seating map is essential.
The EBP Advantage:
The seat selection feature allows attendees to choose their exact seats from an interactive map. It is ideal for auditoriums, seminar halls, cultural programs, theatre shows, and paid performances.
5. Transparent Checkout With Taxes and Fees
Hidden fees frustrate customers. You need clear pricing and a professional checkout flow.
The EBP Advantage:
Event Booking Plus supports ticket pricing, tax setup, service fees, and a clean booking summary. Your customers can see exactly what they are paying before they confirm their booking.
6. Centralized Orders and Attendee Management
After a booking is made, you need to know who booked, how many tickets they purchased, which seats they selected, and what details they submitted.
The EBP Advantage:
The Orders section gives you a complete, searchable list of every attendee, ticket selection, seat information, and payment status. No more digging through emails, spreadsheets, or chat messages.
7. Instant QR Code Check-In
Long queues and paper lists are outdated. QR codes are now a faster and more professional way to manage event entry.
The EBP Advantage:
Every ticket email includes a unique QR code. On the event day, you can scan the code to mark the attendee as present. It is fast, accurate, and creates a professional first impression.
8. Custom Questions and Surveys
Sometimes you need more than a name and email. You may need membership IDs, food preferences, workshop choices, company names, or skill levels.
The EBP Advantage:
Create custom questions and assign them to specific ticket types. All answers are stored in the attendee record, helping you collect useful data and personalize the event experience.

Frequently Asked Questions
1. Is Event Booking Plus truly free for small businesses?
Event Booking Plus offers flexible plans. You can create events and sell tickets with a transparent fee structure. For the latest pricing details or to explore a free trial, please visit the Pricing page or contact the sales team.
2. Can I collect GST or other taxes on my ticket sales?
Yes. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to configure taxes, such as GST, and service fees for events. These charges are calculated and displayed to attendees during checkout.
3. How does the QR code check-in work on the event day?
After attendees book their tickets, they receive an email with a unique QR code. On the event day, you can open the Check-In section in your Event Booking Plus dashboard and scan the QR code using a smartphone or webcam. The system instantly validates the ticket and marks the attendee as present.
4. Can I host events for multiple clients or departments?
Yes. The Organizer Management feature allows admins to create separate organizer profiles for different clients, departments, or teams. Each organizer can have its own events and attendee data, keeping everything organized and easy to manage.
5. What types of events work best with the seat selection feature?
The seat selection feature is ideal for events where assigned seating matters. This includes auditorium events, theatre performances, conference keynote sessions, award ceremonies, cultural programs, and paid shows with fixed seating layouts. You can enable this feature based on the event requirements.

Smarter Event Management in Bangalore with Event Booking Plus
May 25, 2026
Bangalore is a city built on ideas, innovation, networking, and fast-moving business opportunities. From startup meetups and tech conferences to corporate workshops, seminars, product launches, investor events, community gatherings, and auditorium programs, the city has a growing demand for smooth, reliable, and professional event management.
But managing an event successfully is not just about booking a venue and inviting people. Organizers need a system that can handle registrations, ticket sales, attendee details, payments, check-ins, seat selection, communication, and post-event insights without confusion.
That is exactly where
Event Booking Plus
helps.
Event Booking Plus is a complete event management and ticket booking platform that helps organizers manage events from one place, including organizer profiles, event pages, ticket sales, attendee check-ins, payments, customer records, and event data.
A Better Way to Manage Events in Bangalore
Many event organizers still depend on separate tools for registration forms, spreadsheets, payment links, email updates, attendee lists, and check-in management. This may work for a small event, but it quickly becomes difficult when bookings increase or multiple events are being managed at the same time.
Event Booking Plus brings the entire process into one organized platform.
With our platform, organizers can create event pages, manage ticket types, collect attendee information, track bookings, process payments, manage check-ins, and review event performance through a simple dashboard.
For Bangalore-based event organizers, agencies, businesses, startup communities, and professional groups, this means less manual work and better control from planning to event day.
Built for Organizers, Agencies, and Event Teams
Event Booking Plus is designed for people who manage events regularly. Whether you are hosting your own event or managing events for clients, the platform gives you the tools to keep everything structured.
Admins can create and manage organizer profiles with important details such as:
Organizer name
Email address
Organization description
Organization type
Event category
Social media links
Account information
Once an organizer profile is created, their events, tickets, orders, attendees, and activity can be managed from a dedicated dashboard. This is especially useful for event management companies, agencies, and teams handling multiple organizers or clients.
Create Professional Event Pages
Every successful event needs a clear and professional online presence. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to create dedicated event pages that include all the essential details attendees need before booking.
Your event page can include:
Event title
Event description
Start and end date
Venue address
Location details
Maps
Ticket information
Social media links
Booking options
Once the event is created, you can share the event page link through WhatsApp, email, social media, websites, digital ads, or direct campaigns.
This makes promotion easier and gives attendees a smooth path from discovery to booking.
Flexible Ticket Management for Different Event Types
Not every event has the same ticketing needs. A startup meetup may offer free registration. A business conference may have early bird, standard, and VIP tickets. An auditorium event may need seat selection. A workshop may have limited seats.
Event Booking Plus supports flexible ticket setup so organizers can create ticket types based on their event model.
You can manage:
Ticket name
Ticket price
Ticket quantity
Ticket description
Booking start and end dates
Maximum tickets per person
Free ticket options
Paid ticket options
Offline payment options
Seat selection requirements
You can also control when a ticket becomes available for booking. For example, your event page can go live today while ticket sales open next week.
This gives organizers better control over pricing, availability, and registration flow.
Seat Selection for Auditorium and Venue-Based Events
For events that require assigned seating, Event Booking Plus includes seat selection functionality. Attendees can choose their preferred seats from a seating map during the booking process.
This is helpful for:
Auditorium events
Theatre-style programs
Conferences
Seminars
Performances
Large venue-based events
Reserved seating programs
Organizers can structure seating into different sections, helping manage capacity more accurately while giving attendees a better booking experience.
For events that do not require assigned seating, the booking process can remain simple with standard ticket selection.
A Smooth Booking Experience for Attendees
A great event experience starts before the event day. If the booking process is confusing, attendees may drop off before completing registration.
Event Booking Plus is designed to keep the attendee journey simple.
Attendees can:
Open the event page
View event details
Select ticket type
Choose quantity
Select seats, if enabled
Enter attendee details
Answer custom questions, if required
Review the order summary
Complete payment or confirmation
Receive ticket details by email
This clean flow helps attendees register without unnecessary steps, while organizers get accurate booking information in one place.
Secure Checkout, Payments, Fees, and Taxes
Event Booking Plus supports both free and paid events. Organizers can configure ticket prices, platform fees, taxes, and offline payment options based on the needs of the event.
For paid events, attendees can complete checkout online. For free events or offline payment-based events, organizers can confirm bookings without requiring online payment.
The checkout process can show ticket pricing, applicable fees, and taxes where configured, helping attendees understand the final booking amount clearly.
After successful booking, the attendee receives confirmation and ticket details through email.
Manage Orders and Attendee Records in One Place
Once bookings begin, organizers need a clear way to track who registered, what ticket they purchased, whether payment was completed, and whether seats were selected.
The Orders section in Event Booking Plus helps organizers review:
Attendee names
Ticket details
Booking information
Seat selection details
Payment status
Order records
Customer information
This removes the need to manually manage attendee lists in spreadsheets and reduces the risk of missing important booking details.
QR Code Check-In and Attendance Tracking
Event-day check-in can be stressful when attendee lists are long or entry points are crowded. Event Booking Plus helps simplify this with QR code-based check-ins.
After booking, attendees can receive ticket details by email, including QR code information when enabled. At the venue, organizers can scan the ticket QR code and mark the attendee as present.
This helps event teams track:
Who booked tickets
Who attended the event
Ticket type
Seat details
Attendance status
Event turnout
For corporate events, startup events, conferences, training sessions, and auditorium programs, QR-based check-in creates a faster and more organized entry process.
Collect Custom Attendee Information
Different events often need different attendee details. A business event may need company names and job titles. A members-only event may need membership IDs. A training program may need session preferences.
Event Booking Plus allows organizers to add custom questions during the booking process.
You can collect details such as:
Company name
Designation
Membership ID
Food preference
Session preference
Category type
Access requirements
Special instructions
Custom questions can also be assigned to specific ticket types. For example, a member ticket can ask for a membership ID, while a general ticket can ask for basic attendee details.
This gives organizers better information before the event begins.
Event Analytics and Performance Insights
Successful event management does not end when tickets are sold. Organizers need data to understand event performance and improve future planning.
Event Booking Plus helps organizers review useful insights such as ticket sales, attendance records, order details, and event activity.
These insights can help you make smarter decisions about:
Ticket pricing
Promotion strategy
Event capacity
Audience interest
Attendance trends
Future event planning
Venue selection
Registration timing
With better data, every event becomes an opportunity to improve the next one.
Why Bangalore Event Organizers Choose Event Booking Plus
Bangalore’s event ecosystem is fast-paced. Organizers need technology that saves time, improves accuracy, and supports professional event delivery.
Event Booking Plus is a strong solution for:
Startup meetups
Tech conferences
Corporate workshops
Investor events
Product launches
Training sessions
Seminars
Auditorium events
Community programs
Business networking events
With one platform, you can create event pages, sell tickets, collect attendee information, manage payments, enable seat selection, scan QR codes, track attendance, and review event analytics.
Manage Your Next Event with Event Booking Plus
If you are planning an event in Bangalore and want a smarter way to manage registrations, ticketing, payments, attendees, and check-ins, Event Booking Plus is built for you.
Our platform helps you reduce manual work, improve attendee experience, and manage events with confidence from start to finish.
Create your event, manage bookings, track attendees, and deliver a smoother event experience with Event Booking Plus.
FAQs
1. What is Event Booking Plus?
Event Booking Plus is an event management and ticket booking platform that helps organizers create event pages, manage tickets, collect attendee information, process payments, track orders, handle check-ins, and review event performance from one dashboard.
2. Can I use Event Booking Plus for events in Bangalore?
Yes. Event Booking Plus is suitable for Bangalore-based events such as startup meetups, tech conferences, business workshops, seminars, networking events, corporate programs, community events, and auditorium-based events.
3. Does Event Booking Plus support both free and paid events?
Yes. Organizers can create free events, paid events, offline payment events, and ticketed events with different pricing options. Ticket quantities, booking dates, and maximum ticket limits can also be managed.
4. Can attendees choose seats while booking tickets?
Yes. Event Booking Plus supports seat selection for events that require assigned seating. This is useful for auditorium events, conferences, theatre-style programs, and venue-based events with reserved seating.
5. Does Event Booking Plus support QR code check-ins?
Yes. Event Booking Plus supports QR code-based check-ins. Attendees can receive ticket details by email, and organizers can scan the QR code at the venue to mark attendance.

How to Use an Event Planning Website to Streamline Your Guest List
May 5, 2026
Managing an event is exciting, but it can also become overwhelming fast. You are not just choosing a date and inviting people. You are managing registrations, ticket types, attendee details, payments, seating, confirmation emails, guest lists, and check-ins.
When these tasks are handled manually, even a small mistake can create stress. A missed registration, duplicate booking, delayed ticket email, or unclear attendee record can affect the event experience for both organizers and guests.
That is why using an event planning website is no longer just a convenience. It is one of the smartest ways to keep your event organized from the first registration to the final check-in.
Event Booking Plus
, we help organizers manage the full event journey in one place. From creating event pages and selling tickets to tracking attendees and scanning QR codes at entry, our platform is designed to make guest list management easier, faster, and more reliable.
Why Guest List Management Matters More Than You Think
A guest list is more than a list of names. It is the foundation of your event operations.
A well-managed guest list helps you understand:
Who registered for the event
Which ticket type each attendee selected
How many tickets were booked
Whether seat selection is required
Which orders are completed
What attendee details were submitted
Who has checked in on event day
When this information is scattered across emails, spreadsheets, payment apps, and handwritten notes, it becomes harder to manage accurately.
With Event Booking Plus, every booking is automatically connected to your event dashboard. That means attendee information, ticket details, order records, and check-in data stay organized in one central platform.
Start with an Organized Event Setup
Before you can manage a guest list properly, you need a clear event structure.
Event Booking Plus allows admins and organizers to create dedicated organizer profiles. This is especially useful for businesses, associations, event teams, community groups, and professionals who manage multiple events.
Organizer profiles can include:
Organizer name
Email address
Organization description
Organization type
Event category
Social media links
Once the organizer profile is created, events can be added and managed under that organizer’s dashboard. This keeps event data clean, separate, and easy to access.
For teams managing conferences, workshops, seminars, auditorium programs, corporate events, or community gatherings, this structure helps avoid confusion and gives every event its own organized space.
Create Event Pages That Give Attendees Clear Information
Your event page is often the first place attendees go before booking. A strong event page builds confidence and reduces unnecessary questions.
With Event Booking Plus, organizers can create dedicated event pages with important details such as:
Event title
Event description
Start date and time
End date and time
Venue or address
Event status
Ticket options
Seating availability
Location details
Social media links
Once an event is created, it appears as an event card in the dashboard. Organizers can open the event dashboard to manage tickets, orders, attendees, customization, surveys, check-ins, and other settings.
This makes it easier to manage multiple events without mixing up registrations, ticket records, or attendee information.
Build Ticket Types Based on Your Event Needs
Every event is different. Some events need general admission tickets. Others may require VIP passes, member tickets, early-bird pricing, reserved seating, or different access levels.
Event Booking Plus gives organizers flexible ticket management options. You can create ticket types with details such as:
Ticket name
Ticket price
Ticket quantity
Ticket description
Booking availability date
Maximum tickets allowed per attendee
This gives you better control over how tickets are released and how attendees book.
For example, you can schedule tickets to become available on a specific date, limit how many tickets one person can book, or create separate ticket categories for different attendee groups.
This helps prevent overbooking and keeps your guest list accurate from the beginning.
Support Seat Selection for Venue-Based Events
For auditorium events, theatre-style programs, conferences, and hall-based gatherings, seating can be a major part of the attendee experience.
Event Booking Plus supports seat selection for events that require assigned seating. When enabled, attendees can choose their preferred seats from a seating map during the booking process.
This is helpful for:
Auditorium events
Theatre-style programs
Conferences
Seminars
Stage shows
Reserved seating events
For events that do not need assigned seating, organizers can use standard ticket-based entry.
This flexibility makes Event Booking Plus suitable for both simple registration events and structured venue-based events.
Share One Dedicated Event Page URL
Once your event is ready, Event Booking Plus provides a dedicated event page URL that can be shared with your audience.
You can promote your event link through:
Your website
Social media posts
Email campaigns
WhatsApp messages
Digital ads
Direct invitations
Community groups
Attendees can visit the event page, review the details, choose tickets, enter their information, complete payment, and receive their ticket by email.
This creates a smooth booking journey and removes the need for organizers to manually collect registrations one by one.
Collect the Right Attendee Details During Booking
Good guest list management depends on good attendee data.
Event Booking Plus allows attendees to enter their details during the booking process. Organizers can also create custom questions or surveys to collect additional information based on the ticket type.
You may collect details such as:
Contact information
Organization name
Member ID
Special access requirements
Guest preferences
Additional attendee information
Event-specific responses
This helps organizers gather useful information before the event instead of sending separate follow-up forms later.
The collected responses are stored with attendee details, making it easier to prepare for the event and personalize the experience when needed.
Manage Orders and Attendee Records in One Dashboard
After a booking is completed, the order is recorded inside the event dashboard.
The Orders section helps organizers view:
Attendee names
Ticket selections
Seat details, when applicable
Payment status
Booking details
Order records
Custom question responses
This creates a guest list that updates automatically as people register.
Instead of editing spreadsheets every time someone books a ticket, Event Booking Plus records the information for you. This reduces manual work, improves accuracy, and gives organizers a clearer view of event activity.
For teams handling multiple events, this centralized dashboard can save valuable time and reduce last-minute stress.
Send Ticket Emails Automatically
Attendees expect confirmation after they book. If they do not receive a ticket or confirmation email quickly, they may become confused or contact the organizer for support.
Event Booking Plus helps simplify this process by sending ticket details automatically after a successful booking.
The ticket email can include important booking information and QR code details for check-in. This gives attendees confidence that their registration is complete and helps organizers reduce manual follow-up.
A smoother confirmation process creates a better attendee experience before the event even begins.
Speed Up Event Check-In with QR Codes
Check-in is one of the most important moments of the event experience. Long lines, missing names, and unclear records can make an event feel disorganized.
Event Booking Plus supports QR code-based check-ins. On event day, organizers can scan the QR code from an attendee’s ticket and mark them as present.
The check-in section helps organizers track:
Who has arrived
Who has not checked in yet
Which ticket was scanned
Whether a QR code has already been used
Attendance status
This makes entry management faster and more accurate.
For busy events, QR check-in can reduce waiting time, prevent duplicate entry issues, and give organizers real-time visibility into attendance.
Update Event Details Whenever Needed
Event details can change. Timings may shift, venue information may need updating, or descriptions may need edits.
The Customize section in Event Booking Plus allows organizers to update important event details without rebuilding the event from the beginning.
You can adjust event information such as:
Title
Description
Address
Dates
Event settings
Other key details
This helps keep your event page accurate and ensures attendees always see the latest information when they visit the booking page.
A Smarter Way to Manage Your Guest List
Using an event planning website helps organizers move away from scattered manual processes and into a more organized digital workflow.
With Event Booking Plus, you can:
Create organizer profiles
Build dedicated event pages
Manage multiple ticket types
Schedule ticket availability
Enable seat selection
Collect attendee details
Track orders
Send ticket emails
Manage QR code check-ins
View event activity from one dashboard
A successful event depends on more than promotion. It depends on how well registrations, ticketing, attendee records, payments, and check-ins are managed.
Event Booking Plus gives organizers the tools to handle these details with confidence, helping create a smoother experience for attendees and a more organized workflow for event teams.
Ready to Manage Your Next Event More Efficiently?
Your guest list should not be a source of stress. With the right event planning website, you can simplify registrations, reduce manual work, improve check-in speed, and give attendees a professional booking experience.
Event Booking Plus helps you manage everything from one platform — from event setup to final attendance tracking.
Start building your next event with a system designed to keep organizers and attendees connected at every step.
FAQs
1. What is an event planning website?
An event planning website is a digital platform that helps organizers create event pages, manage ticket bookings, collect attendee details, process payments, track orders, and handle check-ins from one place.
2. How does Event Booking Plus help with guest list management?
Event Booking Plus automatically records attendee details when a booking is completed. Organizers can view names, ticket types, seat selections, payment status, order details, and check-in status from the event dashboard.
3. Can I create multiple ticket types in Event Booking Plus?
Yes. Event Booking Plus allows organizers to create multiple ticket types with different names, prices, quantities, descriptions, availability dates, and booking limits.
4. Does Event Booking Plus support seat selection?
Yes. Event Booking Plus supports seat selection for events that require reserved seating. Attendees can choose available seats during the booking process when this option is enabled.
5. How does QR code check-in work?
After booking, attendees receive ticket details by email. On event day, organizers can scan the ticket QR code to verify the attendee and mark them as checked in, making attendance tracking faster and more accurate.
